AUDIT: gheap heap-domain and Default-tail reachability
======================================================================
Questions:
  1. Which static call paths reach the original GameHeap and Default heap allocators?
  2. Which wrappers or vtable entries bypass GameHeap::Allocate after hooks install?
  3. Which constructor/global references can retain a Default heap allocation domain?
